# Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission controller pipeline: the admission.Interface registration, the generic admission chain execution, the mutating admission ordering, and the validating admission webhook call.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

    29→// Attributes is an interface used by AdmissionController to get information about a request
    30→// that is used to make an admission decision.
    31→type Attributes interface {
    32→	// GetName returns the name of the object as presented in the request.  On a CREATE operation, the client
    33→	// may omit name and rely on the server to generate the name.  If that is the case, this method will return
    34→	// the empty string
    35→	GetName() string
    36→	// GetNamespace is the namespace associated with the request (if any)
    37→	GetNamespace() string
    38→	// GetResource is the name of the resource being requested.  This is not the kind.  For example: pods
    39→	GetResource() schema.GroupVersionResource
    40→	// GetSubresource is the name of the subresource being requested.

    17→package admission
    18→
    19→import "context"
    20→
    21→// chainAdmissionHandler is an instance of admission.NamedHandler that performs admission control using
    22→// a chain of admission handlers
    23→type chainAdmissionHandler []Interface
    24→
    25→// NewChainHandler creates a new chain handler from an array of handlers. Used for testing.
    26→func NewChainHandler(handlers ...Interface) chainAdmissionHandler {
    27→	return chainAdmissionHandler(handlers)
    28→}
    29→
    30→// Admit performs an admission control check using a chain of handlers, and returns immediately on first error
    31→func (admissionHandler chainAdmissionHandler) Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error {
    32→	for _, handler := range admissionHandler {
    33→		if !handler.Handles(a.GetOperation()) {
    34→			continue
    35→		}
    36→		if mutator, ok := handler.(MutationInterface); ok {
    37→			err := mutator.Admit(ctx, a, o)
    38→			if err != nil {
    39→				return err
    40→			}
    41→		}
    42→	}
    43→	return nil
    44→}

    31→// Factory is a function that returns an Interface for admission decisions.
    32→// The config parameter provides an io.Reader handler to the factory in
    33→// order to load specific configurations. If no configuration is provided
    34→// the parameter is nil.
    35→type Factory func(config io.Reader) (Interface, error)
    36→
    37→type Plugins struct {
    38→	lock     sync.Mutex
    39→	registry map[string]Factory
    40→}
    41→
    42→func NewPlugins() *Plugins {
    43→	return &Plugins{}
    44→}
    45→

    47→var (
    48→	// PluginEnabledFn checks whether a plugin is enabled.  By default, if you ask about it, it's enabled.
    49→	PluginEnabledFn = func(name string, config io.Reader) bool {
    50→		return true
    51→	}
    52→)

    17→package admission
    18→
    19→import (
    20→	"os"
    21→
    22→	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
    23→
    24→	"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission"
    25→)
    26→
    27→// Config holds the configuration needed to for initialize the admission plugins
    28→type Config struct {
    29→	CloudConfigFile string
    30→}
    31→
    32→// New sets up the plugins and admission start hooks needed for admission
    33→func (c *Config) New() ([]admission.PluginInitializer, error) {
    34→	var cloudConfig []byte
    35→	if c.CloudConfigFile != "" {
    36→		var err error
    37→		cloudConfig, err = os.ReadFile(c.CloudConfigFile)
    38→		if err != nil {
    39→			klog.Fatalf("Error reading from cloud configuration file %s: %#v", c.CloudConfigFile, err)
    40→		}
    41→	}
    42→
    43→	return []admission.PluginInitializer{NewPluginInitializer(cloudConfig)}, nil
    44→}

    21→// newReinvocationHandler creates a handler that wraps the provided admission chain and reinvokes it
    22→// if needed according to re-invocation policy of the webhooks.
    23→func newReinvocationHandler(admissionChain Interface) Interface {
    24→	return &reinvoker{admissionChain}
    25→}
    26→
    27→type reinvoker struct {
    28→	admissionChain Interface
    29→}
    30→
    31→// Admit performs an admission control check using the wrapped admission chain, reinvoking the
    32→// admission chain if needed according to the reinvocation policy.  Plugins are expected to check
    33→// the admission attributes' reinvocation context against their reinvocation policy to decide if
    34→// they should re-run, and to update the reinvocation context if they perform any mutations.
    35→func (r *reinvoker) Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error {
    36→	if mutator, ok := r.admissionChain.(MutationInterface); ok {
    37→		err := mutator.Admit(ctx, a, o)
    38→		if err != nil {
    39→			return e

    43→	return h.operations.Has(string(operation))

    16→
    17→package admission
    18→
    19→type Decorator interface {
    20→	Decorate(handler Interface, name string) Interface
    21→}
    22→
    23→type DecoratorFunc func(handler Interface, name string) Interface
    24→
    25→func (d DecoratorFunc) Decorate(handler Interface, name string) Interface {
    26→	return d(handler, name)
    27→}
    28→
    29→type Decorators []Decorator
    30→
    31→// Decorate applies the decorator in inside-out order, i.e. the first decorator in the slice is first applied to the given handler.
    32→func (d Decorators) Decorate(handler Interface, name string) Interface {
    33→	result := handler
    34→	for _, d := range d {
    35→		result = d.Decorate(result, name)
    36→	}
    37→
    38→	return result
    39→}

Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## Validating Admission Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook]\\n\\n## Kube-apiserver Specific Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. Handlers are ordered by plugin registration, with mutations always before validations\\n\"\n}\n",

Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. Handlers are ordered by plugin registration, with mutations always before validations\\n\"\n}\n",

reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## Validating Admission **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook]\\n\\n## Kube-apiserver Specific Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. packages in kubernetes/kubernetes. Here's the comprehensive flow:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\nThe foundation is defined in **interfaces.go**, which declares three key interfaces:\\n- **Interface**: Base interface with Handles(operation) method\\n- **MutationInterface**: Extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admission\\n- **ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validating admission\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**chain.go** implements the core admission chain:\\n- **chainAdmissionHandler**: A []Interface that processes multiple admission handlers in sequence\\n- **Admit()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Validate()** method: Iterates through handlers, calling Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin factories\\n- **Register()**: Registers plugin factories by name\\n- **NewFromPlugins()**: Builds admission chain from plugin names, separates mutating/validating plugins, wraps with reinvocation handler\\n- Logs loaded plugins in order\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go** implements:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers core API server plugins including lifecycle, webhooks, and admission policies\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go** implements:\\n- **WithStepMetrics()**: Decorator that wraps the admission chain to record admission metrics\\n- Used to track admission latency, rejections, and errors per plugin\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering and Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **mutatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes mutating webhooks, collects patches, applies them to request object\\n- Handles JSON patches from webhooks and mutation audit annotations\\n- Supports re-invocation if mutating webhooks request it\\n\\n## Validating Admission Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to generic webhook dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Admission Policies (CEL-based Rules)\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing MutationInterface\\n- **Admit()** method that delegates to policy dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugin\\n- Evaluates CEL rules to apply mutations using JSONPatch\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **Dispatcher** implementation that evaluates mutating policies\\n- Compiles CEL rules and applies patches to requests\\n- Supports policy composition and ordering\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to policy dispatcher\\n- **Register()** function that registers ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugin\\n- Evaluates CEL rules to validate requests\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **Dispatcher** implementation that evaluates validating policies\\n- Compiles CEL rules and returns validation errors\\n- Supports policy composition and ordering\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook]\\n\\n## Kube-apiserver Specific Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives:\\n1. API server calls AdmissionControl.Admit() on the reinvocation handler\\n2. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n3. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - Mutating webhooks (with parallel execution within each webhook)\\n   - Mutating admission policies\\n4. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed, may re-run mutations\\n5. API server calls AdmissionControl.Validate() on the reinvocation handler\\n6. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n7. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - Validating webhooks (with optional parallel execution)\\n   - Validating admission policies\\n8. Handlers are ordered by plugin registration, with mutations always before validations\\n\"\n}\n",

**ValidationInterface**: Extends Interface with Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validating admission\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**chain.go** implements the core admission chain:\\n- **chainAdmissionHandler**: A []Interface that processes multiple admission handlers in Execution\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go**:\\n- **Plugin** struct implementing ValidationInterface\\n- **Validate()** method that delegates to **validatingDispatcher**: Implements generic.Dispatcher\\n- **Dispatch()** method: Executes validating webhooks in parallel when possible\\n- Returns validation errors without modifying the request\\n- Supports fail-open mode on webhook connection failures\\n\\n## Admission Policies (CEL-based JSONPatch\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- **Dispatcher** implementation that evaluates mutating policies\\n- Compiles CEL rules and returns validation errors\\n- Supports policy composition and ordering\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**:\\n- **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup and Integration\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go**:\\n- **Config** struct has AdmissionControl field (admission.Interface)\\n- AdmissionControl is stored in REST handler context\\n- Used to process all requests through the admission pipeline\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, config file paths, decorators\\n- **ApplyTo()**: Creates admission chain using Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), wraps with metrics decorator, applies it to server config\\n- RecommendedPluginOrder: [NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook]\"\\n\\n## Kube-apiserver Specific Implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go**:\\n- Wraps generic AdmissionOptions with kube-apiserver specific configuration\\n- Delegates to generic ApplyTo() implementation\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go**:\\n- **RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()**: Registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins (21 in-tree plugins)\\n- **AllOrderedPlugins**: Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Comprehensive list defining plugin execution order\\n- **DefaultOffAdmissionPlugins()**: Specifies which plugins are off by default\\n\\n**pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Sets up plugin initializers for dependency injection\\n\\n## Control Plane API Server\\n\\n**pkg/controlplane/apiserver/admission/config.go** and **initializer.go**:\\n- Provides admission configuration for control plane API servers\\n\\n## Metrics and Decorators\\n\\nThe admission chain is wrapped with decorators:\\n- **WithStepMetrics()** (metrics/metrics.go): Records admission latency, rejections, and errors per plugin\\n- Decorators are applied in inside-out order during ApplyTo()\\n- Metrics decorator wraps individual handlers to instrument admission pipeline\\n\\n## Execution Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a request arrives at the API server:\\n1. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Admit() (wrapped by metrics decorator and reinvocation handler)\\n2. Metrics decorator records start time for this step\\n3. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Admit()\\n4. Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - NamespaceLifecycle (namespace existence checks)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based mutation rules)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that mutate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n5. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed:\\n   - If any mutating handler set ShouldReinvoke flag, re-run mutations\\n   - Allows webhooks to react to mutations from other webhooks\\n6. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Validate()\\n7. Metrics decorator records start time for validation step\\n8. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n9. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based validation rules)\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that validate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n10. Metrics decorator records latency and reports success/failure\\n11. Returns to REST handler with admission decision\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Chain of Responsibility**: Multiple handlers form a chain, each can process or reject requests\\n- **Separation of Concerns**: Mutating handlers always run before validating handlers\\n- **Decorator Pattern**: Metrics, decorators wrap handlers to add cross-cutting concerns\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Plugins.Register() and NewFromPlugins() create chains from named plugins\\n- **Reinvocation Policy**: Webhooks can request re-invocation to react to mutations\\n- **Configuration Driven**: Plugins loaded via configuration, not hard-coded\\n\"",

Validate() on ValidationInterface handlers, returning on first error\\n- **Handles()** method: Returns true if any handler handles the operation\\n\\n**reinvocation.go** wraps the chain to support reinvocation:\\n- **newReinvocationHandler()**: Creates a wrapper that can reinvoke the admission chain if webhooks request re-invocation\\n- Checks reinvocation context after Admit() to determine if second pass is needed\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/)\\n\\n**plugins.go** implements:\\n- **Plugins** struct: Registry of admission plugin **Webhook** struct: Base implementation for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- Manages webhook configuration sources, HTTP client, namespace/object matchers\\n- Implements ValidateInitialization() to ensure proper setup\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/configuration_manager.go**:\\n- Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** and **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager**: Lister-based managers for webhooks\\n\\n## API Server Setup and context\\n- Used to process all requests through the admission pipeline\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go**:\\n- **AdmissionOptions** struct holds plugin names, Chain iterates through all registered mutating handlers in order:\\n   - NamespaceLifecycle (namespace existence checks)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based mutation rules)\\n   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that mutate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n5. Reinvoker checks if reinvocation is needed:\\n   - If any mutating handler set ShouldReinvoke flag, re-run mutations\\n   - Allows webhooks to react to mutations from other webhooks\\n6. REST handler calls AdmissionControl.Validate()\\n7. Metrics decorator records start time for validation step\\n8. Reinvoker delegates to chainAdmissionHandler.Validate()\\n9. Chain iterates through all registered validating handlers in order:\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based validation rules)\\n   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (webhooks that validate requests)\\n   - Each handler is wrapped by metrics decorator\\n10. Metrics decorator records latency and reports success/failure\\n11. Returns to REST handler with admission decision\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Chain of Responsibility**: Multiple handlers form a chain, each can process or reject requests\\n- **Separation of Concerns**: Mutating handlers always run before validating handlers\\n- **Decorator Pattern**: Metrics, decorators wrap handlers to add cross-cutting concerns\\n- **Factory Pattern**: Plugins.Register() and NewFromPlugins() create chains from named plugins\\n- **Reinvocation Policy**: Webhooks can request re-invocation to react to mutations\\n- **Configuration Driven**: Plugins loaded via configuration, not hard-coded\\n\"\n}\n",
